&q;,&q;url&q;:&q;https://www.thefelixstoweapp.com/blog/i/49983671/felixstowe-artist-ashley-peck-painting-war-time-aircraft&q;,&q;images&q;:[{&q;id&q;:&q;img-49983671-38709058&q;,&q;url&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/default/49983671-38709058.jpg?v=1600710994&q;,&q;otherImagesUrl&q;:{&q;large&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/grande/49983671-38709058.jpg?v=1600710994&q;}},{&q;id&q;:&q;img-49983671-38709062&q;,&q;url&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/default/49983671-38709062.jpg?v=1600711013&q;,&q;otherImagesUrl&q;:{&q;large&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/grande/49983671-38709062.jpg?v=1600711012&q;}}],&q;isFeatured&q;:&q;img-49983671-38709058&q;,&q;smallThumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/resizeapi/1f9d12f9c72b9290ec7f43f6ac602af84590de8c/157/93/&q;,&q;thumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/resizeapi/1f9d12f9c72b9290ec7f43f6ac602af84590de8c/314/196/&q;,&q;originalThumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/grande/49983671-38709058.jpg?v=1600710994&q;,&q;largeThumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/resizeapi/1f9d12f9c72b9290ec7f43f6ac602af84590de8c/750/-1/&q;,&q;xLargeThumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/resizeapi/1f9d12f9c72b9290ec7f43f6ac602af84590de8c/1200/-1/&q;,&q;xxLargeThumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/resizeapi/1f9d12f9c72b9290ec7f43f6ac602af84590de8c/3200/-1/&q;,&q;latitude&q;:&q;0&q;,&q;longitude&q;:&q;0&q;,&q;subtitle&q;:&q;&q;,&q;isHeadline&q;:0,&q;authorAvatarUrl&q;:&q;&q;,&q;meta&q;:{&q;title&q;:&q;&q;,&q;description&q;:&q;&q;},&q;commentsEnabled&q;:true,&q;commentsPostUrl&q;:&q;https://www.thefelixstoweapp.com/apiv3/submitComment/37517446/49983671/?username=[name]&a;comment=[content]&a;email=[email]&q;,&q;commentsUrl&q;:&q;https://www.thefelixstoweapp.com/apiv3/getCommentsByItem/37517446/49983671/1/24/&q;,&q;nbcomments&q;:0,&q;subsections&q;:{&q;37517446&q;:[&q;LOCAL PEOPLE&q;,&q;LOCAL HISTORY&q;,&q;ARTS, THEATRE &a; MUSIC&q;,&q;RECENTLY ADDED&q;]}},{&q;type&q;:&q;article&q;,&q;subtype&q;:&q;mcms&q;,&q;id&q;:49835565,&q;author&q;:&q;&q;,&q;title&q;:&q;Felixstowe\xe2\x80\x99s Alternative - Folk Singer/Songwriter, Belinda Gillett&q;,&q;date&q;:&q;2020-08-02T19:27:00+02:00&q;,&q;leadin&q;:&q;&q;,&q;summary&q;:&q;As a little girl, I loved music, dancing and singing but it wasn\xe2\x80\x99t until we came to Felixstowe that it became my passion. When I was nine we spent a summer living at the local caravan park, where they held a talent competition every week, which I entered and won first time. In fact, I won every week until I was asked politely not to enter anymore to \xe2\x80\x98give the others a chance\xe2\x80\x99. At this point my mother took me to perform in local shows, such as the Dennis Lowe productions and Felixstowe Musical Theatre at the Spa Pavilion, then branching out to perform at the Wolsey and Theatre Royal Norwich. By the time I was thirteen I had done some TV work, including singing on BBC\xe2\x80\x99s Going Live.This inevitably gained me some new friends at high school, which pushed me on further. In the summer of that same year I won the chance to make a record with Brian May and spent the next year on a promotional tour around the country, singing on radio and TV. It was an amazing time, but showed me that\xe2\x80\xa6&q;,&q;content&q;:&q; &l;div class=\\&q;photo top\\&q; style=\\&q;text-align:center\\&q;&g; &l;a href=\\&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/grande/49835565-38641673.jpg?v=1600191459\\&q; target=\\&q;_blank\\&q;&g; &l;img id=\\&q;img-49835565-38641673\\&q; src=\\&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/default/49835565-38641673.jpg?v=1600191460\\&q; alt=\\&q;Felixstowe\xe2\x80\x99s Alternative - Folk Singer/Songwriter, Belinda Gillett\\&q; title=\\&q;Felixstowe\xe2\x80\x99s Alternative - Folk Singer/Songwriter, Belinda Gillett\\&q; /&g; &l;/a&g; &l;/div&g; &l;br class=\\&q;clear\\&q; /&g; &l;div class=\\&q;texte\\&q; &g; &l;p&g;As a little girl, I loved music, dancing and singing but it wasn\xe2\x80\x99t until we came to Felixstowe that it became my passion. When I was nine we spent a summer living at the local caravan park, where they held a talent competition every week, which I entered and won first time. In fact, I won every week until I was asked politely not to enter anymore to \xe2\x80\x98give the others a chance\xe2\x80\x99. At this point my mother took me to perform in local shows, such as the Dennis Lowe productions and Felixstowe Musical Theatre at the Spa Pavilion, then branching out to perform at the Wolsey and Theatre Royal Norwich. By the time I was thirteen I had done some TV work, including singing on BBC\xe2\x80\x99s Going Live.This inevitably gained me some new friends at high school, which pushed me on further. In the summer of that same year I won the chance to make a record with Brian May and spent the next year on a promotional tour around the country, singing on radio and TV. It was an amazing time, but showed me that fame was not something I was sure was meant for me, particularly as in my teen years I started to experience mental health issues that would continue throughout my adult life. This led to my decision to decline an offer at stage school and other professional singing work, and I started my vocal training and went back to the quiet life in Felixstowe.&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;The next creative break through came when I learnt to play guitar at twenty-one. I fell instantly in love with making music and writing my own songs, and apart from a long break to raise my children, I have continued ever since.&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;For the last 15 years I have immersed myself in the art of songwriting and performing. I studied Fine Art at Norwich University College of the Arts which helped me explore my creativity. I spent a few years playing festivals, in London and all over the country, gaining interest from record companies that, again, I felt I wasn\xe2\x80\x99t able to pursue. I took a long break and now, in the last two years have been performing again from a far more confident and settled place. I love playing locally and some favourites have been Folkeast, Ipswich Music Day and Cambridge Folk Club.&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;I have released four albums and EPs on the Ipswich label Backwater Records, which supports local musicians. Now that lockdown has ended, I have resumed recording my next album which I hope to release early next year. I still also paint when I can. Felixstowe is a wonderful place to be inspired by.I write plenty of songs walking the fields and the beaches and as such, my music is heavily based around the nature and landscapes of Suffolk. I hope to continue contributing to the local scene and encourage young musicians to develop their talents and get out and perform.&a;nbsp;&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;If you\xe2\x80\x99d like to listen to my music, here are some useful links for you:&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;&l;a href=\\&q;https://backwaterrecords.com/belindagillett\\&q;&g;https://backwaterrecords.com/belindagillett&l;/a&g;&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;&l;a href=\\&q;https://open.spotify.com/artist/16KTBvHSVEVzJVt3LedWNq\\&q;&g;https://open.spotify.com/artist/16KTBvHSVEVzJVt3LedWNq&l;/a&g;&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;&l;a href=\\&q;https://www.instagram.com/belindagillettmusic/?hl=en\\&q;&g;https://www.instagram.com/belindagillettmusic/?hl=en&l;/a&g;&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;Wishing you all well, Belinda&l;/p&g; &l;div class=\\&q;_1GmxSv9K16\\&q; style=\\&q;font-weight: inherit; position: absolute; bottom: 0px; left: 0px; width: 0px; height: 0px; transform-origin: left top; box-sizing: border-box; transform: scale(1.39657);\\&q;&g;&a;nbsp;&l;/div&g; &l;/div&g; &l;br class=\\&q;clear\\&q; /&g; &l;div class=\\&q;photo top\\&q; style=\\&q;text-align:center\\&q;&g; &l;a title=\\&q;Felixstowe\xe2\x80\x99s Alternative - Folk Singer/Songwriter, Belinda Gillett\\&q; /&g; &l;/a&g; &l;/div&g; &l;br class=\\&q;clear\\&q; /&g; &l;div class=\\&q;photo top\\&q; style=\\&q;text-align:center\\&q;&g; &l;a href=\\&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/grande/49835565-38641681.jpg?v=1600191499\\&q; target=\\&q;_blank\\&q;&g; &l;img id=\\&q;img-49835565-38641681\\&q; src=\\&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/default/49835565-38641681.jpg?v=1600191500\\&q; alt=\\&q;Felixstowe\xe2\x80\x99s Alternative - Folk Singer/Songwriter, Belinda Gillett\\&q; title=\\&q;Felixstowe\xe2\x80\x99s Alternative - Folk Singer/Songwriter, Belinda Gillett\\&q; /&g; &l;/a&g; &l;/div&g; &l;br class=\\&q;clear\\&q; /&g; &q;,&q;url&q;:&q;https://www.thefelixstoweapp.com/blog/i/49835565/felixstowe-s-alternative-folk-singer-songwriter-belinda-gillett&q;,&q;images&q;:[{&q;id&q;:&q;img-49835565-38641673&q;,&q;url&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/default/49835565-38641673.jpg?v=1600191460&q;,&q;otherImagesUrl&q;:{&q;large&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/grande/49835565-38641673.jpg?v=1600191459&q;}},{&q;id&q;:&q;img-49835565-38641680&q;,&q;url&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/default/49835565-38641680.jpg?v=1600191481&q;,&q;otherImagesUrl&q;:{&q;large&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/grande/49835565-38641680.jpg?v=1600191481&q;}},{&q;id&q;:&q;img-49835565-38641681&q;,&q;url&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/default/49835565-38641681.jpg?v=1600191500&q;,&q;otherImagesUrl&q;:{&q;large&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/grande/49835565-38641681.jpg?v=1600191499&q;}}],&q;isFeatured&q;:&q;img-49835565-38641673&q;,&q;smallThumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/resizeapi/a38d466474b036950e7a9491e27da0716152a72e/157/93/&q;,&q;thumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/resizeapi/a38d466474b036950e7a9491e27da0716152a72e/314/196/&q;,&q;originalThumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/grande/49835565-38641673.jpg?v=1600191459&q;,&q;largeThumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/resizeapi/a38d466474b036950e7a9491e27da0716152a72e/750/-1/&q;,&q;xLargeThumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/resizeapi/a38d466474b036950e7a9491e27da0716152a72e/1200/-1/&q;,&q;xxLargeThumbnail&q;:&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/resizeapi/a38d466474b036950e7a9491e27da0716152a72e/3200/-1/&q;,&q;latitude&q;:&q;0&q;,&q;longitude&q;:&q;0&q;,&q;subtitle&q;:&q;&q;,&q;isHeadline&q;:0,&q;authorAvatarUrl&q;:&q;&q;,&q;meta&q;:{&q;title&q;:&q;&q;,&q;description&q;:&q;&q;},&q;commentsEnabled&q;:true,&q;commentsPostUrl&q;:&q;https://www.thefelixstoweapp.com/apiv3/submitComment/37517446/49835565/?username=[name]&a;comment=[content]&a;email=[email]&q;,&q;commentsUrl&q;:&q;https://www.thefelixstoweapp.com/apiv3/getCommentsByItem/37517446/49835565/1/24/&q;,&q;nbcomments&q;:0,&q;subsections&q;:{&q;37517446&q;:[&q;RECENTLY ADDED&q;,&q;ARTS, THEATRE &a; MUSIC&q;]}},{&q;type&q;:&q;article&q;,&q;subtype&q;:&q;mcms&q;,&q;id&q;:49937275,&q;author&q;:&q;&q;,&q;title&q;:&q;YOU PROTECT ME AND I PROTECT YOU&q;,&q;date&q;:&q;2020-08-01T20:28:00+02:00&q;,&q;leadin&q;:&q;&q;,&q;summary&q;:&q;It seems an awfully long time since we locked down back in the middle of March. Like millions of others I suddenly found myself unable to work as my housekeeping business came almost to a stop within a matter of days and I suddenly found myself with a lot more time on my hands.&q;,&q;content&q;:&q; &l;div class=\\&q;texte\\&q; &g; &l;p&g;It seems an awfully long time since we locked down back in the middle of March. Like millions of others I suddenly found myself unable to work as my housekeeping business came almost to a stop within a matter of days and I suddenly found myself with a lot more time on my hands.&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;The debate on the merits and pitfalls of wearing masks (or face coverings) had barely begun at this stage as countries everywhere tried various ways to reduce the spread of infection. Here in t he UK the government quite rightly decided, on the evidence it had, to protect the NHS supply lines by not asking people to wear masks.&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;We felt however that wearing a homemade mask was a sensible compromise, leaving medical masks for the healthcare professionals whilst adding an extra physical barrier to the social distancing and hand washing measures already in place. On a borrowed sewing machine, we started making masks for family and friends out of old bedding and t-shirts. Word got out and people we di dn\xe2\x80\x99t even know started to give us material and equipment in exchange for some masks and we were soon able to provide masks to organisations such as care homes, the BASIC Life Charity shop in Walton and even to Ipswich Hospital for staff to use whilst off duty.&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;Demand increased quickly when many people found us via the amazing Facebook page: &l;a href=\\&q;https://www.facebook.com/search/top?q=felixstowe%20helping%20hands\\&q;&g;Felixstowe Helping Hands&l;/a&g;. This is a group of exceptional people whose sole purpose is to help and support the community in any way that it can. We\xe2\x80\x99re very fortunate to have such good people here in Felixstowe.&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;Around the end of May we stopped using old materials and the masks we have made since are all produced from two or three layers of 100% cotton purchased online in a variety of colours and designs. We started to charge \xc2\xa32.50 to cover the cost of materials and equipment as well as taking 50 pence for ourselves (for each hour we give to the project we produce only around six or seven masks). We later added a further 50p to raise a few pounds for NHS charities and the East Anglian Childrens Hospice, so thank you for nearly \xc2\xa3400 to date.&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;As they became an increasing part of daily life, there is now an endless supply of good quality masks at reasonable prices both online and in the high street, which is great news for everyone as they may well be with us for a long time to come. It\xe2\x80\x99s worth remembering that wearing a mask arguably protects others from you more than it does you from them so if we both mask up, as the young lady on Youtube said back in March, \xe2\x80\x9cYou protect me and I protect you\xe2\x80\x9d.&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;As we are now back to working full - time, we are now focusing on producing a small number of matching \xe2\x80\x9cshopping kits\xe2\x80\x9d comprising a folding shopping bag with two face masks all in a smaller zipped and lined bag that doubles as a cosme tic bag in your choice of material. You can see these at our Facebook page,&l;a href=\\&q;https://www.facebook.com/Felixstowe-Face-Masks-104016321402862\\&q;&g; Felixstowe Face Masks&l;/a&g;. Please let us know if you would like one.&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;Finally, thank you to all who helped, especially in the early days. We\xe2\x80\x99ve met some wonderful people along the way and we hope you all stay safe and well. Now go wash your hands!&l;/p&g; &l;p&g;Written by Ivana&a;nbsp;Majerikova&l;/p&g; &l;/div&g; &l;br class=\\&q;clear\\&q; /&g; &l;div class=\\&q;photo top\\&q; style=\\&q;text-align:center\\&q;&g; &l;a src=\\&q;https://cmsphoto.ww-cdn.com/superstatic/2348751/art/default/49937275-38690294.jpg?v=1600540810\\&q; alt=\\&q;YOU PROTECT ME AND I PROTECT YOU\\&q; title=\\&q;YOU PROTECT ME AND I PROTECT YOU\\&q; /&g; &l;/a&g; &l;/div&g; &l;br class=\\&q;clear\\&q; /&g; &l;div class=\\&q;photo top\\&q; style=\\&q;text-align:center\\&q;&g; &l;a
